[2023-05-17 16:51:20][base_learner.py:338][INFO] [RANK0]: DI-engine DRL Policy
MAVAC(
  (actor_encoder): Identity()
  (critic_encoder): Identity()
  (critic_head): Sequential(
    (0): Linear(in_features=111, out_features=512, bias=True)
    (1): ReLU()
    (2): RegressionHead(
      (main): Sequential(
        (0): Linear(in_features=512, out_features=512, bias=True)
        (1): ReLU()
      )
      (last): Linear(in_features=512, out_features=1, bias=True)
    )
  )
  (actor_head): Sequential(
    (0): Linear(in_features=54, out_features=256, bias=True)
    (1): ReLU()
    (2): ReparameterizationHead(
      (main): Sequential(
        (0): Linear(in_features=256, out_features=256, bias=True)
        (1): ReLU()
        (2): Linear(in_features=256, out_features=256, bias=True)
        (3): ReLU()
      )
      (mu): Linear(in_features=256, out_features=4, bias=True)
    )
  )
  (actor): ModuleList(
    (0): Identity()
    (1): Sequential(
      (0): Linear(in_features=54, out_features=256, bias=True)
      (1): ReLU()
      (2): ReparameterizationHead(
        (main): Sequential(
          (0): Linear(in_features=256, out_features=256, bias=True)
          (1): ReLU()
          (2): Linear(in_features=256, out_features=256, bias=True)
          (3): ReLU()
        )
        (mu): Linear(in_features=256, out_features=4, bias=True)
      )
    )
  )
  (critic): ModuleList(
    (0): Identity()
    (1): Sequential(
      (0): Linear(in_features=111, out_features=512, bias=True)
      (1): ReLU()
      (2): RegressionHead(
        (main): Sequential(
          (0): Linear(in_features=512, out_features=512, bias=True)
          (1): ReLU()
        )
        (last): Linear(in_features=512, out_features=1, bias=True)
      )
    )
  )
)
